 23 writers, including Ramdarsha Mishra in Hindi, Shamim Tariq in Urdu and Cyrus Mistry in English, have been announced to be honored with the country's prestigious Sahitya Akademi Award this year
 sahitya academy ke sachiv ke
 Srinivasan Rao told a press conference that this year it has been decided to give Sahitya Akademi Award to six poetry collections, six story collections, four novels, two essay collections, two plays, two critiques and one memoir
 unhone bataaya ki academy dwaara diya jane vaala bhashaa sammaan saal 2014 ke liye shrikant bahulkar ko diya jayega
 He said that it was decided to award Mishra for his collection of poems 'agni Ki Laughter', while Tariq would be given the award for his critique 'tasavvuf and Bhakti'
 angreji ke upanyaas 'chronical of e corps bearar' ke liye mistre ko puraskaar se nawaja jayega
 Rao said that it has been decided to award the award for 23 Indian languages in the executive board meeting held on Thursday under the chairmanship of Akademi President Vishwanath Prasad Tiwari, while the award for Bangla language will be announced later
 academy ke sachiv ne bataaya ki rajasthani or punjabi main mudh acharya 'ashaavadi' or jasvindar singh ko unke upanyaas kramash:, 'gavaad' or 'maat lok' ke liye puraskaar diya jayega, jabaki maithili main manmohan jha ko unki kahani 'khissa', sanskrit main ramshankar avasthi ko unke kavita sangrah 'vanadevi' ke liye puraskaar se nawaja jayega
 He said that the announced litterateurs would be presented with awards at the FICCI auditorium on February 16 next year

 Secretary of Sahitya Academy
 shrinivasana raav ne samvaadadaata sammelan main bataaya ki is saal chah kavita sangrah, chah kahani-sangrah, chaar upanyaas, do niabandh-sangrah, do naatak, do samalochna or ek sansmaran ko sahitya academy puraskaar dene kaa faisla kiya gaya he
 He said that the language honor given by the academy will be given to Srikant Bahulkar for the year 2014
 unhone kaha ki mishra ko unki kavita sangrah 'aag kii hansi' ke liye puraskaar dene kaa nirnay kiya gaya, jabaki tarik ko unki samalochna 'tasawwuf or bhakthi' ke liye puraskaar diya jayega
 Mistry will be awarded the award for the English novel 'chronicle of a Corps Bearer'

 The academy's secretary said that in Rajasthani and Punjabi, Mudha Acharya 'ashavadi' and Jaswinder Singh would be awarded for their novels, 'gawad' and 'maat Lok' respectively, while Manmohan Jha in Maithili was given the story 'khissa', In Sanskrit, Ramshankar Awasthi will be awarded the award for his collection of poems 'vanadevi'

 bijepi likhit aashwaasan dene ke paksh main to katai nahin he
 2
 jammu-kashmir main afaspa [AFSPA - sashastr bal visheshadhikaar kanoon] ko lekar donon partiyon kii alag alag raay rahi he
 bjp's stand is that the opinion of the army should be taken in this and since it is the privilege of the center, this matter should be left to the central government
 pidipi kii maang rahi he ki is par pakistan se baatcheet kerani chahie
 3
 mukhyamantri kis kaa hoga? ab is par vivaad nahin rah gaya he
 It has been decided that Mufti Mohammad Sayeed will be the Chief Minister from PDP winning more seats
 isi tarah bijepi bijepi ke nirmal singh up mukhyamantri kii kursi sanbhaalenge, ye bhi takreeban tay hi he
 The PDP wants Saeed to remain Chief Minister for a full six years, while the BJP wants both parties to hold the post of Chief Minister for three-three years
 4
 The stand of BJP and PDP has also been conflicting over talks with Pakistan and Hurriyat on Kashmir issue, but after talks between Prime Minister Narendra Modi and Pakistani Prime Minister Nawaz Sharif, both sides are being soft on the matter
 5
 The political interests of both are clinging to the status quo and the Delimitation Commission for refugees from Pakistan
 is par baatcheet se rasta nikaalane kii koshish he
 Apart from these, the PDP wants free trade and tourism between Jammu and Kashmir and Pakistan Occupied Kashmir, the return of Kashmiri youths lodged in jails outside the state, to give Srinagar and Dal Lake World Heritage status under the central government's '100 Smart Cities'
 
 vaise aisa lag rahaa he ki donon partiyaan vivaadaaspad muddon ko zyada tool na dete hue bich kaa rasta talash rahi hai
 In this connection, two conversations have been held between PDP patron Mufti Muhammad Saeed and Prime Minister Narendra Modi - now the two are just meeting face to face
 isi saal janvari main hue pathankot hamale par enie ne mohali kii special court main 101 pannon kii chargeshit daakhil kii he
 The charge sheet includes jaish-e-mohammed commander Maulana Masood Azhar, his brother Abdul Rauf Asghar, launching commander Shahid Latif and handler Kasif Jan as the main accused
 chargeshit main enie ne bataaya he ki kis tarah masood ajahar ne janvari main pathankot airbase par hamale kii sajeesh rachi thi
 The purpose of the attack was to kill Air Force personnel and destroy the entire airbase, including the weapons and other military goods there
 bataa den ki pakistan ke rahane vaale nasir hossain, abu bakar, umr farrukh or abdul kayum naam ke chaar fidaayin aatankwaadiyon ne ek janvari, 2016 kii raat pathankot airbase par hamalaa kiya tha
 Seven soldiers were killed in this attack, while 37 people were injured
 jaaniye, enie kii chargeshit kii 10 badi baaten
 1
 jaish sargana masood ajahar, dipti chif rauf asagar, lonching commander shahid latif or handler kashif jaan ne apane aakaaon ke saath milakar hamale kii puri sajeesh rachi thi
 2
 chargeshit main enie ne bataaya he kipthankot hamaleke liye aatankiyon ko kahaan or kaise pakistan-afghanistan border par training di gai thi
 3
 aatankiyon ne airbase se phone par apane handlers se baat kii thi
 In which a terrorist talks to his mother through his handlers
 saath hi maa ko airbase ke andar maujuudagi kii jaankaree bhi detaa he
 4
 aatankiyon ne pakistan main baithe apane handlers ashfak ahamed or abdul shakur se bhi baat kii thi
 They are also named in the charge sheet
 5
 The terrorists had earlier booked a Toyota Innova taxi through their handlers
 taxi driver ko pakistan ke number se phone aayaa tha
 The driver was asked to reach an area of pathankot in Punjabi
 6
 Four terrorists were sitting in a booked taxi from the area
 ve taxi ko ek behad kharaab raste se le gaye
 The path was so bad that the rim of the Innova car was broken
 jiske baadaaatankiyonne taxi ko akalgarh main chhod diya tha
 7
 taxi kharaab hone ke baad unhone ek esayuvi car ko roka
 Incidentally, in this car, SP Salvinder Singh of Gurdaspur was seated
 aatankiyon ne salwinder, unke dost or cook ko kidanap kar liya
 The militants had snatched Salvinder's phone
 8
 An officer's guard called on this phone
 phone aatankiyon ne uthaaya or assalaam alaikum kaha
 The guard said talk to SP sir
 isi hadabadi main aatankiyon ne phone kaata or salwindar ko kuch kimi dur chhod diya gaya
 9
 chargeshit main shaamil kiye gaye aatankiyon main se teen aatanki masood ajahar, rouf or shahid latif ke khilaaf red corner notice jari kiya ja chukaa he
 The process of issuing a Red Corner Notice against Kashif Jaan is underway
 10
 Kashif Jaan was also talking to the terrorists and was giving all the information from these 3 mobile numbers to Jaish's bosses
 ye pakistani number the- 923453030479, 923213132786 or 923017775253
 Let us tell you that after the charge sheet, it is believed that the Government of India can put more pressure through the United Nations to declare Samsood Azhar an 'international terrorist'
 gauratlab he, bharat sarkaar iske liye kai baar koshish kar chuki he, par har baar china bharat kii koshish par pani pher detaa tha
 After the Pathankot attack, the NIA has now given full information about Masood Azhar and his terrorist accomplices in court along with all the evidence
 star ballebaaj mitali raaj kii naabad ardhshtkeey pari or priyanka raay kii shandaar gendbaaji se bhartiya mahila team ne westeindies ko tisare or antim twanti-20 antarrashtriya cricket match main 15 ran se haraakar siries 2-1 se jiti
 Batting first after winning the toss, the Indian team scored 128 runs for five wickets thanks to an unbeaten 51 off Mithali's 46-ball three fours
 westeindies kii team iske jawaab main nau wicket par 113 ran hi bana pai
 From her side, only Stacy Ann King (37) could stand up to the bowlers
 bharat kii taraf se priyanka ne 17 ran dekar teen or sonia dabir ne 10 ran dekar do wicket liye

 westeindies kii taraf se shemeni campbell ne 20 ran dekar teen wicket liye

 usne iske baad bhi niyamit antaraal main wicket ganvaae
 Apart from King, only Shanele Dele (19), Deandra Dotin (18) and Pearl Ateney (11 not out) reached double digits for her side
 bhartiya mahila team ne isse pehle westeindies se ekadivasiy siries 3-2 se jiti thi
 The government-appointed committee on Friday to investigate the lobbying activities of Walmart stores in the US to gain entry into the Indian market met the executives of the global retail chain and sought details
 samiti kii wallmart asia tathaa bharti samooh ke saath uski sanyukt udhyam company bharti wallmart privet limited ke pratinidhiyon se mulaakaat hui
 Representatives were also accompanied by their lawyers on the occasion
 company se samiti dwaara puche gaye sawaalon kaa byora dene ko kaha gaya tha
 The committee was set up by Walmart to investigate reports of American lawmakers engaging in lobbying activities to gain entry into the rapidly growing Indian market
 samiti jaanch kar rahi he ki walmart ne kya kisi bhartiya kanoon kaa ulanghan karte hue bharat main aisi koi gatividhi chalaane kii koshish kii he
 The committee will also investigate other matters related to this issue
